<script>
(function(){
    var isDebug = false;
    var debug = isDebug ? console.log : function(){};

    var gaLayer;
    if(!window.gtmDataLayer && ! window.dataLayer){
        gaLayer = window.gtmDataLayer  = window.dataLayer = []
    } else {
        gaLayer = window.gtmDataLayer ||  window.dataLayer;
    }
    debug('ICU:gaLayer -- data:', gaLayer);

    function encase(fn, x) {
        try {
            return fn(x);
        } catch(err) {
            return null;
        }
    }

    function getCookie(name) {
        var list = (document.cookie)
            .split('; ')
            .filter(function(s) { return s.includes(name + '='); })
            .map(function(s) { return s.slice((name + '=').length); });
        return encase(JSON.parse, encase(window.atob, list[0] || null));
    }

    function uuidv4() {
        return 'xxxxxxxx-xxxx-4xxx-yxxx-xxxxxxxxxxxx'.replace(/[xy]/g, function(c) {
            var r = Math.random() * 16 | 0, v = c == 'x' ? r : (r & 0x3 | 0x8);
            return v.toString(16);
        });
    }

    // Get ICU cookie
    var icuCookie = getCookie('icu');
    debug('ICU:icuCookie -- data:', icuCookie);

    // Check if cookie has fingerprint
    var fingerprint = icuCookie && icuCookie['fingerprint'] || null;
    debug('ICU:fingerprint -- data:', fingerprint);

    // Check if cookie has gusID
    var gusID = icuCookie && icuCookie['gus_id'] || null;
    debug('ICU:gusID -- data:', gusID);

    // Check if cookie has global_fingerprint
    var global_fingerprint = icuCookie && icuCookie['global_fingerprint'] || 'ffp-' + uuidv4();
    debug('ICU:global_fingerprint -- data:', global_fingerprint);

    // Create new data
    var data = Object.assign({},
        { fingerprint: fingerprint || global_fingerprint },
        { global_fingerprint: global_fingerprint },
        gusID ? { gus_id: gusID } : null
    );
    debug('ICU:data -- data:', data);

    // Push ga data to gaLayer
    gaLayer.push({
        'event': 'purch_icu',
        'datas': data
    });
    debug('ICU:gaLayer -- data:', gaLayer);

    // Set cookie with updated data
    var newCookie = Object.assign({}, icuCookie, data);
    document.cookie = 'icu=' + window.btoa(JSON.stringify(newCookie));
    debug('ICU:newCookie -- data:', newCookie);

    // Load icu.js file
    var s=document.createElement('script');
    s.type='text/javascript';
    s.defer = true;
    s.src ='//assets.purch.com/loe/icu/1.0.1-35/icu.js';
    s.addEventListener('load', async function() {
        // When icu.js is loaded, call ICU function with config
        Purch.cs_extradata = Purch.cs_extradata || {};

        function sleep(ms) { return new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, ms)) }

        async function isGaLoaded() {
            let i = 0;
            while (typeof ga === "undefined" && i < 3) {
                i = i + 1;
                await sleep(1000);
            }
            return ga;
        }

        async function isTmnLoaded() {
            let i = 0;
            while (typeof tmntag.pubtargets === "undefined" && i < 3) {
                i = i + 1;
                await sleep(1000);
            }
            return tmntag;

        }

        // need to wait until ga and tmntags have been loaded
        var gaObject = await isGaLoaded();
        var tmnTag = await isTmnLoaded();

        window.ICU({
            debug: isDebug,
            tmnTag: tmnTag,
            gaObject: gaObject,
            dataLayers: [ Purch.cs_extradata || []],
            gaDataLayer: window.gtmDataLayer ||  window.dataLayer || [],
        });
    });
    document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(s);
})();

<script type="text/javascript">
    (function(){
        // hasProperty :: a -> String -> Bool
        const hasProperty = obj => key => Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(obj, key);

        // isObject :: a -> Bool
        const isObject = val => typeof val === 'object';

        // merge :: a -> b -> c
        const merge = obj1 => (obj2) => {
            const obj = Object.assign({}, obj1);
            let key;
            for (key in obj2) {
                if (key === '__proto__' && !hasProperty(obj1)(key)) {
                    continue;
                }

                let oldVal = obj1[key];
                let newVal = obj2[key];

                if (Array.isArray(oldVal) && Array.isArray(newVal)) {
                    obj[key] = oldVal.concat(newVal);
                } else if (isObject(oldVal) && isObject(newVal)) {
                    obj[key] = merge(oldVal)(newVal);
                } else {
                    obj[key] = newVal;
                }
            }

            return obj;
        };


        var config = merge({
            html_content: {
                subTitle : 'Your membership helps us deliver great news and content.',
                formButton: 'Join Now',
            },
